Friday, May 11, 2018, from 10 a.m. to 1 p.m., School Counselors from all high schools in Baltimore City will host the Reach Higher Baltimore Signing day event at the Royal Farms Arena.  This event is for ALL SENIORS, not just those who are planning to go to college. Students must arrive and leave on the buses with their schools. Lunch will be provided at no cost to students. Several local college representatives will be present. In addition, we have put together a fantastic line up of entertainers, DJ’s and local radio personalities to join in and celebrate the success of Baltimore City seniors. Parents/guardians are invited.  Each student will receive one (1) guest ticket.
